Where you collect, process or disclose Precise Location Data for Cross-App Advertising from a mobile application, you shall ensure that such mobile application prominently posts notice to End Users: (a) that End Users precise geolocation data may be shared with third parties; and (b) the purposes for which such data may be used, including Cross-App Advertising.  Precise Location Data means any information that identifies or is capable of determining with reasonable specificity the actual physical location of an End User or device (e.g., GPS level latitude/longitude coordinates, location-based Wi-Fi triangulation or cellular tower data).  Cross-App Advertising as currently defined by the Network Advertising Initiative (NAI), means the collection of data through applications owned or operated by different entities on a particular device for the purpose of delivering advertising based on the preferences or interests known or inferred from the data collected, or as may be amended by the NAI from time to time.

13.4	Opt-Out Mechanism. For purposes of this Agreement, the Opt-Out Mechanism on a mobile application will be a description of how an End User can access a privacy device setting (e.g., Apple iOS Limit Ad Tracking).

13.5	Precise Location.  If you collect, process or disclose Precise Location Data from a mobile application, then: (a) you shall ensure that the such mobile application obtains express (i.e., opt-in) consent from End Users; and (b) the applicable mobile applications privacy policy must disclose such information collection, processing or disclosure.  Where you collect, process or disclose Precise Location Data for Cross-App Advertising from a mobile application, you shall ensure that such mobile application prominently posts notice to End Users: (a) that End Users precise geolocation data may be shared with third parties; and (b) the purposes for which such data may be used, including Cross-App Advertising.  Precise Location Data means any information that identifies or is capable of determining with reasonable specificity the actual physical location of an End User or device (e.g., GPS level latitude/longitude coordinates, location-based Wi-Fi triangulation or cellular tower data).  Cross-App Advertising as currently defined by the Network Advertising Initiative (NAI), means the collection of data through applications owned or operated by different entities on a particular device for the purpose of delivering advertising based on the preferences or interests known or inferred from the data collected, or as may be amended by the NAI from time to time.

Precise Location Data means any information that identifies or is capable of determining with reasonable specificity the actual physical location of an End User or device (e.g., GPS level latitude/longitude coordinates, location-based Wi-Fi triangulation or cellular tower data).  Cross-App Advertising as currently defined by the Network Advertising Initiative (NAI), means the collection of data through applications owned or operated by different entities on a particular device for the purpose of delivering advertising based on the preferences or interests known or inferred from the data collected, or as may be amended by the NAI from time to time.

Precise Location Data means any information that identifies or is capable of determining with reasonable specificity the actual physical location of an End User or device (e.g., GPS level latitude/longitude coordinates, location-based Wi-Fi triangulation or cellular tower data).  Cross-App Advertising as currently defined by the Network Advertising Initiative (NAI), means the collection of data through applications owned or operated by different entities on a particular device for the purpose of delivering advertising based on the preferences or interests known or inferred from the data collected, or as may be amended by the NAI from time to time.

Such notice to End Users of your mobile applications shall be provided anywhere the applications may be acquired and prior to installation of the applications (e.g., Apple App Store or Google Play Store), or websites where the mobile applications are acquired. 

13.4	Opt-Out Mechanism. For purposes of this Agreement, the Opt-Out Mechanism on a mobile application will be a description of how an End User can access a privacy device setting (e.g., Apple iOS Limit Ad Tracking).

13.5	Precise Location.  If you collect, process or disclose Precise Location Data from a mobile application, then: (a) you shall ensure that the such mobile application obtains express (i.e., opt-in) consent from End Users; and (b) the applicable mobile applications privacy policy must disclose such information collection, processing or disclosure.  Where you collect, process or disclose Precise Location Data for Cross-App Advertising from a mobile application, you shall ensure that such mobile application prominently posts notice to End Users: (a) that End Users precise geolocation data may be shared with third parties; and (b) the purposes for which such data may be used, including Cross-App Advertising.  Precise Location Data means any information that identifies or is capable of determining with reasonable specificity the actual physical location of an End User or device (e.g., GPS level latitude/longitude coordinates, location-based Wi-Fi triangulation or cellular tower data).  Cross-App Advertising as currently defined by the Network Advertising Initiative (NAI), means the collection of data through applications owned or operated by different entities on a particular device for the purpose of delivering advertising based on the preferences or interests known or inferred from the data collected, or as may be amended by the NAI from time to time.

13.5	Precise Location.  If you collect, process or disclose Precise Location Data from a mobile application, then: (a) you shall ensure that the such mobile application obtains express (i.e., opt-in) consent from End Users; and (b) the applicable mobile applications privacy policy must disclose such information collection, processing or disclosure.  Where you collect, process or disclose Precise Location Data for Cross-App Advertising from a mobile application, you shall ensure that such mobile application prominently posts notice to End Users: (a) that End Users precise geolocation data may be shared with third parties; and (b) the purposes for which such data may be used, including Cross-App Advertising.  Precise Location Data means any information that identifies or is capable of determining with reasonable specificity the actual physical location of an End User or device (e.g., GPS level latitude/longitude coordinates, location-based Wi-Fi triangulation or cellular tower data).  Cross-App Advertising as currently defined by the Network Advertising Initiative (NAI), means the collection of data through applications owned or operated by different entities on a particular device for the purpose of delivering advertising based on the preferences or interests known or inferred from the data collected, or as may be amended by the NAI from time to time.

Where you collect, process or disclose Precise Location Data for Cross-App Advertising from a mobile application, you shall ensure that such mobile application prominently posts notice to End Users: (a) that End Users precise geolocation data may be shared with third parties; and (b) the purposes for which such data may be used, including Cross-App Advertising.  Precise Location Data means any information that identifies or is capable of determining with reasonable specificity the actual physical location of an End User or device (e.g., GPS level latitude/longitude coordinates, location-based Wi-Fi triangulation or cellular tower data).  Cross-App Advertising as currently defined by the Network Advertising Initiative (NAI), means the collection of data through applications owned or operated by different entities on a particular device for the purpose of delivering advertising based on the preferences or interests known or inferred from the data collected, or as may be amended by the NAI from time to time.

13.5	Precise Location.  If you collect, process or disclose Precise Location Data from a mobile application, then: (a) you shall ensure that the such mobile application obtains express (i.e., opt-in) consent from End Users; and (b) the applicable mobile applications privacy policy must disclose such information collection, processing or disclosure.  Where you collect, process or disclose Precise Location Data for Cross-App Advertising from a mobile application, you shall ensure that such mobile application prominently posts notice to End Users: (a) that End Users precise geolocation data may be shared with third parties; and (b) the purposes for which such data may be used, including Cross-App Advertising.  Precise Location Data means any information that identifies or is capable of determining with reasonable specificity the actual physical location of an End User or device (e.g., GPS level latitude/longitude coordinates, location-based Wi-Fi triangulation or cellular tower data).  Cross-App Advertising as currently defined by the Network Advertising Initiative (NAI), means the collection of data through applications owned or operated by different entities on a particular device for the purpose of delivering advertising based on the preferences or interests known or inferred from the data collected, or as may be amended by the NAI from time to time.

Precise Location Data means any information that identifies or is capable of determining with reasonable specificity the actual physical location of an End User or device (e.g., GPS level latitude/longitude coordinates, location-based Wi-Fi triangulation or cellular tower data).  Cross-App Advertising as currently defined by the Network Advertising Initiative (NAI), means the collection of data through applications owned or operated by different entities on a particular device for the purpose of delivering advertising based on the preferences or interests known or inferred from the data collected, or as may be amended by the NAI from time to time.

Cross-App Advertising as currently defined by the Network Advertising Initiative (NAI), means the collection of data through applications owned or operated by different entities on a particular device for the purpose of delivering advertising based on the preferences or interests known or inferred from the data collected, or as may be amended by the NAI from time to time.

Precise Location Data means any information that identifies or is capable of determining with reasonable specificity the actual physical location of an End User or device (e.g., GPS level latitude/longitude coordinates, location-based Wi-Fi triangulation or cellular tower data).  Cross-App Advertising as currently defined by the Network Advertising Initiative (NAI), means the collection of data through applications owned or operated by different entities on a particular device for the purpose of delivering advertising based on the preferences or interests known or inferred from the data collected, or as may be amended by the NAI from time to time.

Precise Location Data means any information that identifies or is capable of determining with reasonable specificity the actual physical location of an End User or device (e.g., GPS level latitude/longitude coordinates, location-based Wi-Fi triangulation or cellular tower data).  Cross-App Advertising as currently defined by the Network Advertising Initiative (NAI), means the collection of data through applications owned or operated by different entities on a particular device for the purpose of delivering advertising based on the preferences or interests known or inferred from the data collected, or as may be amended by the NAI from time to time.
